<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шушукаться.html>шушу́каться</a> (22532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic; from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шу.html>шу</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:шу.html>шу</a>!</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šu, šu!</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shhh!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-katʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">шушу́кати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šušúkaty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">шушу́каць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šušúkacʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">шу́шкаць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šúškacʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">шушу́кам</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šušúkam</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">шу̏шкати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rustle, to make noise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">шу́штати</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">šȗškati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rustle, to make noise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.
</p>

***шхуна.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шхуна.html>шху́на</a> (9330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schoener</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шхуна.html>шху́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šxúna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шхуна.html>шху́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шхуна.html>шху́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шхуна.html>шху́н</a></b>)

***щадить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щадить.html>щади́ть</a> (8954)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">щадѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščaděti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to keep, spare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ščęditi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*skend-</i>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скудный.html>ску́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skúdnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щадить.html>щади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощадить.html>пощади́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spare, to have mercy (on)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:щадить.html>щади́ть</a></b> чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ščadítʹ</b> čʹí-libo čúvstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to spare</b> somebody's feelings</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспощадный.html>беспоща́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bespoščádnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">неща́дный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neščádnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощада.html>поща́да</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poščáda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щадить.html>щадя́щий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ščadjáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щебень.html>ще́бень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščébenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щебень.html>ще́бня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щебень.html>ще́бни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щебень.html>ще́бней</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щебетать.html>щебета́ть</a> (16904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щебет.html>ще́бет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščébet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щебетать.html>щебета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščebetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to twitter, to chirp</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chatter, to prattle</li></ol>

***щеголь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щеголь.html>щёголь</a> (24035)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear; perhaps related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">щего́л</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščegól</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">goldfinch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szczególny</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">special, particular</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щеголь.html>щёголь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščógolʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щеголь.html>щёголя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щеголь.html>щёголи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щеголь.html>щёголей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dandy, fop, beau</li>
<li>spotted redshank, spotshank (<i>Tringa erythropus</i>)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щеголять.html>щеголя́ть</a> (17078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щеголь.html>щёголь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščógolʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щеголять.html>щеголя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščegoljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">щегольну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress like a dandy, to wear fancy clothes</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flaunt <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sport <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***щедрый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щедрый.html>ще́дрый</a> (7514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">штедръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štedrŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ščedrъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szczodry</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σκεδάννῡμι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skedánnūmi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I split or scatter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щедрый.html>ще́дрый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščédryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)щедре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)щедре́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>generous <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">willing to give and share unsparingly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:великодушный.html>великоду́шный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">velikodúšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bogátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обильный.html>оби́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obílʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобильный.html>изоби́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izobílʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щедрость.html>ще́дрость</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ščédrostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***щека.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a> (984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">шчака́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščaká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">щока́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščoká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a> *ščeka. 
</p><p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščeká</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щеки́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёк</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cheek
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a> (кого́-либо) <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щеке́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">udáritʹ (kovó-libo) po <b>ščeké</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slap (smb.) in the face</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поцеловать.html>поцелова́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́бе</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pocelovátʹ v óbe <b>ščóki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kiss both cheeks</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>При</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́че</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поцеловать.html>поцелова́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́бе</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pri vstréče oná menjá pocelovála v óbe <b>ščóki</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">When we met, she kissed me on both cheeks.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впалый.html>впа́лые</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vpályje <b>ščóki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sunken cheeks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подставить.html>подста́вить</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podstávitʹ <b>ščóku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn the cheek</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razduvátʹ <b>ščóki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to puff out the cheeks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:румянец.html>румя́нец</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rumjánec vo vsju <b>ščóku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><i>red in the cheeks</i> (said when one is shy)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">упи́сывать <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́бе</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щеки́</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">upísyvatʹ za óbe <b>ščekí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to eat heartily, to gobble</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щеко́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za čužój <b>ščekój</b> zub ne bolít</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you cannot feel another’s toothache</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́ми</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́ми</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужи́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержи́шь</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za svoími <b>ščekámi</b> ne uderžál, za čužími ne uderžíšʹ</i></dd><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">if you can’t keep it under your own cheeks, you won’t be able to keep it under someone else’s</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mouth <span class="use-with-mention">of animals</span>, jaw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбий.html>ры́бья</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rýbʹja <b>ščeká</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fish’s mouth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> side, sidepiece, stock, jaw (of a mechanism)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a></b> дроби́лки</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ščeká</b> drobílki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">crushing jaw</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коленчатый.html>коле́нчатого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вал.html>ва́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ščeká</b> kolénčatovo vála</i> ― <span class="e-translation">crankshaft web</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a></b> кривоши́па</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ščeká</b> krivošípa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">web</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***щекотавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щекотавший.html>щекота́вший</a> (11206)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***щекотать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:щекотать.html>щекота́ть</a> (11206)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">скъкътати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skŭkŭtati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щекотать.html>щекота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščekotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пощекотать.html>пощекота́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">защекота́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tickle, to titillate (touch repeatedly or stroke delicately)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chirp, to twitter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">said of nightingales, magpies and certain other birds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">защекота́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaščekotátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щекотать.html>щекота́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščekotátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щекотливый.html>щекотли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ščekotlívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)щекотли́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)щекотли́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>delicate, touchy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">requiring great circumspection and tact</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:щекотливый.html>щекотли́вое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ščekotlívoje</b> položénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>delicate/touchy</b> situation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ticklish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> extremely scrupulous</li></ol>
